You open your eyes to towering aisles of toys and hear the faint sound of a [[baby|Baby 1]] crying. \n\n//A superhero action figure!//\n"Dad? Can you buy me this? Please?"\n"No, son, let's go. We don't have time for this"\n"Please dad?"\n"I said no. Now come on."\n\n[[{Put it in your pocket}|Steal]]\n[[{Put it back on the shelf}|Don't Steal]]\n\n\n
[10:13 pm Mom:] Are you almost here? \n[10:14 pm You:] On my way...\n\n[[{Send}|send]]\n\n
You follow the nurse down the hall to the nursery and look through the window. She point's at one of the babies.\n"That's your little girl," she says.\nDespite everything, you smile.\n\n[[In the end, something turned out okay.|End]]
Quickly, while your father's back is turned, you stuff the action figure into your pocket. \nAs you run to catch up to him, somebody yells, "Hey! Put that back!"\nFear strikes you.\nWorkers start to walk towards you. Everybody is staring.\nBlood begins to drip down your face. Your head begins to feel light and your vision blurs.\n\nYou have died.
